 exact (univalent_iso_comma F G).
  
C‚ÇÅ, C‚ÇÇ, C‚ÇÉ: bicat_of_univ_cats

‚ñπ pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G) = Œ≤

      apply iso_comma_ump2_pr2.
    Qed.
  End CellUMP.

‚ñπ pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G) = Œ≤
 exact (pb_ump_2_nat_trans_pr2 œÜ œà Œ± Œ≤ r).
  Defined.

  Context {C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ : bicat_of_univ_cats}

    := total_univalent_category D‚ÇÇ.

    := pr1_category _.

    := total_functor (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F D‚ÇÇ).

  (œÄ‚ÇÅ ¬∑ F) (œÄ‚ÇÇ ¬∑ pr1_category D‚ÇÇ)

  (pr1_category D‚ÇÇ
   :
   bicat_of_univ_cats ‚ü¶ tot_D‚ÇÇ, C‚ÇÇ ‚üß)

 exact reindexing_has_pb_ump_1.
    
C‚ÇÅ, C‚ÇÇ: bicat_of_univ_cats

  Section CellUMP.
    Let p := comma_comma_cone.

    F ‚Ä¢ (Œ± ‚ñπ F))
 ‚Ä¢ rassociator œà (comma_cone_pr1 comma_comma_cone)
     F) ‚Ä¢ (œà ‚óÉ comma_cone_cell comma_comma_cone)
comma_ump_2_nat_trans œÜ œà Œ± Œ≤ r
‚ñπ comma_cone_pr2 comma_comma_cone = Œ≤
 exact (comma_ump_2_nat_trans_pr2 œÜ œà Œ± Œ≤ r).
  Defined.

End CommaObject.

  : has_comma bicat_of_univ_cats
  := Œª C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ C‚ÇÉ F G, comma_comma_cone F G ,, comma_has_ump F G.

End EquifiersCat.

      ¬∑ iso_inserter_cone_pr1
          (iso_inserter_cone_bicat_of_univ_cats F G))

   (functor_to_cat_iso_inserter

         (iso_inserter_cone_cell q)))
   (iso_inserter_cone_pr1
      (iso_inserter_cone_bicat_of_univ_cats F G)) F
 ‚Ä¢ (nat_z_iso_to_invertible_2cell
      (functor_to_cat_iso_inserter
         (iso_inserter_cone_pr1 q)

‚Ä¢ iso_inserter_cone_cell q
 abstract
      (use nat_trans_eq ; [ apply homset_property | ] ;
       intro x ; cbn ;
       rewrite (functor_id F), (functor_id G) ;
       rewrite !id_left, !id_right ;
       apply idpath).
